. I'm not thrilled with the hot sauce they put on the side though, so I suggest offering more alternatives for that.  This place is very close to Home Depot and American Tire. A good place to go while waiting on your tire to get fixed. There's also a Walmart across the street.< /review>< pictures>

<Text>Visited the newly opened Bascom Branch Library now that the Grand Opening hype has died down.  Instead opted to come on a Family Activity night to check it out after work and what a treat it was.  While the Family activity event is geared towards younger kids, maybe 2-5, the overall atmosphere was fantastic for a Wednesday evening.  The librarians were helpful, knowledgeable and friendly and not at all disconnected like several i have met at other libraries we frequent.

The facilities are amazing, with a grand attrium as we entered leading to the community center/fitness center on one side and teh Library on the other.  Inside, the library was mostly spacious and well lit at night.  A safe children's area fo rthe young ones, a dedicated teen room, computers in the tech center and both quiet study and group study rooms surround the the main stacks in the middle.

<Name>Jaspal Kaur< /Name>< Time>
1570339552443<//Time>
<rate>5<//rate>< review>
All religions have temples where people can gather together to contemplate on God and pray. The Sikh temple is called a Gurdwara. The word 'Gurdwara' means 'Gateway to the Guru'. In Sikhism ones personal dedication to living a good life is important but another important aspect of Sikhism is the Sangat (congregation). Not only should one meditate on God on their individual level but also on a corporate level. There are thousands of Gurdwaras throughout Punjab and the rest of the world. They serve as community centers for the Sikh's. There are no restrictions on who may enter a Gurdwara for prayer. People of all religions are welcome to attend. Another common feature of all Gurdwaras around the world is Langar, the free community kitchen. Here food is served to all people who sit together to enjoy a communal meal. It is a symbol of the Sikh belief in a non-sexist, non-racist society where all people of all casts, religions are equal and can share a common meal in the true spirit of unity.<//review>

I don't know where to start because I have so many good things to say! We had our first visit this week (which was a free temperament test to make sure the dog is non-aggressive), and I was really blown away by my experience. Not only is the website awesome (you create an account and can purchase packages, make visit reservations, view photos/updates of your dog, etc.), but everyone I interacted with was so kind and dog-loving, and it was clear from chatting with them that they all had met and interacted with my dog that day.

The report card for his temperament test was really detailed and so sweet and positive. Made me really proud of my pup. :) They included a bunch of pictures as well so I could see how he was doing and other dogs he was meeting. The next day they also posted a welcome message on their Facebook account with a collage of my dog! Such a cute extra touch.

Before coming here, I had been becoming more and more uncomfortable with taking my dog to the dog park (I've seen some really sketchy things go down there, including when a dog tried to kill another dog!). So I really appreciate how strict they are about vaccinations and with requiring a temperament test for every new dog. It makes me feel more comfortable knowing that every dog my boy will interact with has been vetted!

The only minor complaint I have was that my pup has smelled fairly strongly of perfume for the last few days since his visit... Although, since this likely means he was getting lots of love from a staff member, I suppose I can't complain too much! :)

This place is great! It is very reasonably priced for the location and the food is good too. Located on the end of the Malibu pier, this restaurant has indoor, outdoor, and rooftop seating with panoramic ocean views. The atmosphere is causal and laid back. You order at the counter and the food is brought to your table. In my experience the food came out very quickly. The only negative is the lack of parking (street or expensive lot), so it is best to make it part of a Malibu beach day. With the prime location, good food, and reasonable prices, I can‚Äôt think of a better lunch spot in the area. (The picture is the fried egg sandwich)
